簡單易用的介面，可順暢切換多樣的編輯作業。\r\n* 全功能的相片編輯器，讓您美化相片並使想像力成真。\r\n\r\n裁切：\r\n\r\n* 迅速修飾相片—裁切、拉直、順時針與逆時針旋轉、水平與垂直翻轉。\r\n\r\n* 裁切也提供簡單的單指預設長寬比例。\r\n\r\n修正：\r\n\r\n以簡單的滑桿即讓相片脫穎而出：\r\n\r\n* 控制並設定對比、清晰度、飽和度、鮮豔度、除霧化\r\n透過這些控制項，於相片中創造驚人的效果。\r\n對比是極為吸睛的控制項，能讓普通相片轉為眩目傑作。\r\n除霧化滑桿可為相片新增或移除霧化效果。\r\n調整清晰度滑桿，調整相片的質感與細節。\r\n除霧化滑桿可為相片新增或移除霧化效果。\r\n\r\n* 曝光、重點動態、陰影、黑與白\r\n您可調整曝光度，進而微調相片的曝光設定。重點動態與陰影，能最佳化您相片曝光的的重點動態、中間影調 (明度)、陰影，且不致影響其他區域的色調。\r\n「黑與白」可設定相片的黑點與白點。如此可讓更多色彩完全以黑或白呈現。\r\n\r\n* 色溫與色調\r\n色溫與色調可為您的相片加入暖色或冷色。您也可控制相片中綠色與紅色色調的多寡。\r\n以「色溫」滑桿增加或降低橙色或藍色色調的多寡。增加橙色色調，讓相片呈現更溫暖的感覺。增加藍色色調，讓相片呈現更冷冽的感覺。\r\n以「色調」滑桿為相片增加更多紅色或綠色色調。自動白平衡可為您自動調整。\r\n\r\n* 詳細資訊\r\n銳化、減少明度噪訊、減少色彩噪訊，都可讓相片看來更漂亮，同時儘可能消除相片裡不需要的顆粒與斑點。\r\n\r\n* 分色調\r\n透過亮部與陰影的色調，風格化您的照片。\r\n\r\n* 漸淡\r\n以全新的「漸淡效果」將影像與背景融合，並創造出相片霧面的感覺。\r\n\r\n*暈影效果\r\n以暈影效果讓您的影像添增感傷或觸動懷舊的情懷。\r\n\r\n點部修復\r\n* 移除斑點或污漬從未如此輕鬆！在您的相片按一下即移除痘痘、疤痕、灰塵。\r\n\r\n移除紅眼及修正寵物眼：\r\n\r\n* 輕點一下即可移除相片中人物或寵物的紅眼。\r\n您可使用「紅眼」工具減去相片中的紅眼。如此能降低目標區域的紅色像素飽合度，減輕紅眼效應。\r\n\r\n自動修正：\r\n\r\n* 輕點一下即自動調整，藉以編輯您的相片。\r\n\r\n支援 raw 相片：\r\n* Write music, using your digital pen*, and StaffPad will transform your handwritten notation into a beautifully typeset score which you can then edit, play back, print and share. For composers and musicians, StaffPad revolutionises the art of writing music.\r\n\r\n*IMPORTANT NOTE: STAFFPAD **REQUIRES** A DEVICE WITH ACTIVE PEN CAPABILITIES. As you move from bar to bar, StaffPad will convert your handwriting into a beautifully engraved score. You can draw notes, beams, stems, articulations, accidentals, slurs, ties and more. It’s the most natural way to write music on digital device, ever.\r\n\r\nAN ORCHESTRA IN THE TIP OF YOUR PEN\r\nStaffPad contains a bespoke playback engine, and an entire orchestra which has been meticulously recorded and programmed to play back your score with incredible realism. Multiple dynamics layers, multiple recorded articulations, repetition samples and smart playback rules ensure that what you see is what you hear. The entire symphony orchestra is represented, and more instruments are available to purchase from the in-app store.\r\n\r\nStaffPad is powerful. Everything from a basic piano lead sheet to a full symphony score can be written with StaffPad.\r\n\r\nA BEAUTIFUL EXPERIENCE\r\nWriting music should be the focus of a composer. StaffPad handles everything else for you whilst you work. The interface has been designed to reduce clutter, and is context sensitive - showing only the information you want, when you want it.\r\n\r\nPEN AND TOUCH\r\nBy combining the power of digital inking and multitouch, we can offer a no-compromises approach to virtual manuscript. Use your finger to move around the score, and pinch to zoom - with butter-smooth scrolling. When you want to write music, just use the pen. Use your eraser button on the pen to remove both ink strokes and existing notation. You can also draw freehand on the score, using the sketch layer, to quickly brainstorm and leave notes/comments for yourself and others.\r\n\r\nPRINT YOUR RESULTS\r\nStaffPad will intelligently layout the score when it’s time to print. You can print the entire score, as well as individual parts for each musician. You can export MIDI and MusicXML, should you wish to continue working on your score in other programs. StaffPad also supports import of MusicXML and MIDI files.\r\n\r\nSCORE SYNC AND AUTO-SAVE\r\nStaffPad is always saving your score, and keeping track of versions - which you can return to at anytime. By saving your scores to OneDrive, you can ensure that your scores are kept in sync across all your devices. StaffPad also syncs your settings and preferences. Currently, the voice assistant is available in US and UK English only.\r\n\r\nEXPRESS YOURSELF\r\nStaffPad is the first notation application which allows you to easily draw dynamics/music expression data right onto the staff.
